## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P. This is a classic population dynamics ODE problem where the growth rate typically depends on current population through density-dependent feedback mechanisms, and may include explicit time dependence for environmental forcing or non-autonomous dynamics.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (strong Allee effect with minimum viable population)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (c2 + P) (growth enhanced at intermediate densities)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolic minus catabolic scaling)
- Seasonally forced logistic: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (periodic environmental variation)
- Time-dependent growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) * P (exponentially changing growth rate)
- Richards growth model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible sigmoidal growth)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (higher-order density effects)
- Logarithmic correction: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * P * log(P) (log-modified logistic)
- Rational density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (growth rate saturating at high density)
- Harvesting/immigration model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 (logistic with constant immigration or harvesting)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope Ôćĺ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects Ôćĺ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay Ôćĺ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior Ôćĺ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects Ôćĺ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent feedback Ôćĺ multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) representing carrying capacity limitation
- Allee effects (positive density dependence at low P) Ôćĺ additional multiplicative factor (P - c) creating a growth threshold
- Per-capita growth rate declining linearly with P Ôćĺ dP/dt is quadratic in P (logistic-type parabola)
- Environmental periodicity Ôćĺ multiplicative sinusoidal modulation sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) on growth parameters
- Metabolic scaling in growth Ôćĺ difference of power laws: c0*P^a - c1*P^b with different exponents for anabolism vs catabolism
- Logarithmic growth regulation Ôćĺ Gompertz-type log(c/P) factor indicating multiplicative rather than additive density feedback
- Constant term independent of P Ôćĺ represents immigration, stocking, or constant harvesting rate
- Rational saturation in per-capita rate Ôćĺ P/(1+c*P) form indicating resource competition or handling time effects

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG6)
============================================================
GT: -c0*c1*P + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P**c6 + c7*P
Candidate formulas: 50

I need to first simplify the Ground Truth expression to understand what function it represents.

**GT numerical expression:**
`-6.216849410245645*1.4127513976416965*P + 0.8578822735168387*(1 - P/79.20259671838578)*P + 0.8578822735168387*P**0.333333333333333 + 0.8578822735168387*P`

Let me compute the coefficients:
- First term: -6.216849 * 1.412751 * P Ôëł -8.7834 * P
- Second term: 0.85788 * (1 - P/79.2026) * P = 0.85788*P - 0.85788/79.2026 * P┬▓ Ôëł 0.85788*P - 0.010831*P┬▓
- Third term: 0.85788 * P^(1/3)
- Fourth term: 0.85788 * P

Combining P terms: (-8.7834 + 0.85788 + 0.85788)*P = -7.0677*P
P┬▓ term: -0.010831*P┬▓
P^(1/3) term: 0.85788*P^(1/3)

So GT Ôëł **-0.010831*P┬▓ - 7.0677*P + 0.85788*P^(1/3)**

Note: No constant term, no dependence on t.

Now I need a candidate that can express: `c_a * P┬▓ + c_b * P + c_c * P^(1/3)` (with no constant term, no t-dependence).

Let me check candidates:

**Candidate 49**: `P**(1/4) + P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + c3 + c4/P**(1/3)`
This has P^(1/4) fixed (coefficient 1), not P^(1/3). Can't match.

**Candidate 18**: `P**(1/4) + P**2*c0 + P*c1 + c2 + c3/P**(1/3)`
Has P^(1/4) and P^(-1/3), not P^(1/3). Can't match.

**Candidate 36**: `P**c0*c1 + P**c2*c3 + c4`
Setting c0=2, c2=1/3: c1*P┬▓ + c3*P^(1/3) + c4. Missing the linear P term. Can't match (need 3 power terms).

**Candidate 37**: `P*c0 + P*c1*log(P*c2 + 1) + P*c3 + P**c4 + P**c5*c6 + c7`
Set c1=0 (kills log term), c4=2 gives P^2 but coefficient is 1. Not flexible. Set c5=2, c6=..., c4=1/3. Then: P*(c0+c3) + P^(1/3) + c6*P^2 + c7. Need c7=0. This gives P^(1/3) with coefficient 1, but GT needs 0.85788. The P^(1/3) has fixed coefficient 1... Wait, P**c4 has coefficient 1. Set c4=1/3: coefficient is 1, not 0.85788.

But set c5=1/3, c6=0.85788, and c4=2 (coefficient 1 for P^2, but GT needs -0.01083). P**c4 = P^2 with coefficient 1 ÔÇö can't adjust.

**Candidate 40**: `P**2*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3/(c4 + t)**5 + P**c5 + c6`
Set c3=0 (kills t-dependence), c5=1/3. Then: c0*P┬▓ + (c1+c2)*P + P^(1/3) + c6. Need c6=0. P^(1/3) has coefficient 1, but GT needs 0.85788. Can't adjust.

**Candidate 30**: `P**3*c0*t**c1 + P**3*c2 + P**2*c3 + P**2*c4 + P*c5 + P*c6 + P**c7 + c8`
Set c0=0 (kills t), c2=0, c7=1/3. Then: (c3+c4)*P┬▓ + (c5+c6)*P + P^(1/3) + c8. P^(1/3) coefficient is 1, need 0.85788. Can't adjust.

**Candidate 32**: `P*c0 + P*c1 + P**c2 + P**c3*c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7`
Set c5=0, c2=2, c3=1/3. Then: (c0+c1)*P + P┬▓ + c4*P^(1/3) + c7. P┬▓ has coefficient 1, need -0.01083. Can't adjust.

None of the candidates can produce exactly `a*P┬▓ + b*P + c*P^(1/3)` with all three coefficients free.

GT Equivalence Verification (BPG6)
============================================================
GT: -c0*c1*P + c2*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*P**c6 + c7*P
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) simplifies to a function of **P only**:
\[
-6.2168\cdot 1.41275\,P \;+\;0.857882(1-\tfrac{P}{79.2026})P \;+\;0.857882\,P^{1/3}\;+\;0.857882\,P
\]
Expand the quadratic term:
\[
0.857882(1-\tfrac{P}{79.2026})P = 0.857882\,P - \frac{0.857882}{79.2026}P^2
\]
So GT is exactly of the form
\[
\text{GT}(P)= A\,P^2 + B\,P + C\,P^{1/3}
\]
with **no constant term**, no \(P^{1/4}\), and no \(P^{-1/3}\), and **no dependence on \(t\)**.

A candidate can match only if, after choosing its constants (and possibly restricting domain), it can reduce to exactly \(A P^2 + B P + C P^{1/3}\).

---

### Candidate-by-candidate analysis

1. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + \frac{P c1}{c2 t + c3} + c4 + \frac{c5}{c2 t + c3} + \frac{c6}{P^{1/3}}\)  
   Has unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) term (fixed coefficient 1) and \(t\)-dependence unless forced away; also has \(P^{-1/3}\). Cannot become \(A P^2 + B P + C P^{1/3}\). **No**.

2. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + P c2 + P^{c3} c4 + c5 + c6/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). Also extra constant \(c5\) can be set 0 but \(P^{1/4}\) cannot. **No**.

3. \(P^{1/5} + P c0 + P c1 + P + P^{c2} c3 + c4 + c5/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/5}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

4. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2/t^5 + c3 + c4/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\); also \(t\)-term unless \(c2=0\). Still **No**.

5. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3 e^{c4\sin(P c5 + c6)} + c7/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). Exponential-sine term can be killed by \(c3=0\) but still **No**.

6. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3 \frac{t}{c4 t + c5} + \frac{c6}{c4 t + c5} + c7/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\), \(P^{-1/3}\), and \(t\)-dependence unless \(c3=c6=0\). Still **No**.

7. \(P c0 + P^{c1} + c2 + c3 e^{P c4}\log(P c5 + 1) + c6/P^{1/3}\)  
   Has \(P^{-1/3}\) unless \(c6=0\). But then still has \(P^{c1}\) with implicit coefficient 1 (cannot scale), and no way to create both \(P^2\) and \(P^{1/3}\) simultaneously (only one power term). Also log-exp term must be removed via \(c3=0\). Still cannot match GTÔÇÖs three-term structure. **No**.

8. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + P c2 + P c3 + c4 + c5/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

9. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + P c1 e^{P c2} + c3 + c4/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

10. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + \frac{P c2}{P c3 + 1} + c4 + c5/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). Rational term canÔÇÖt become polynomial globally. **No**.

11. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3 t (P+c4)^{c5} + c6/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\), \(P^{-1/3}\), and \(t\)-dependence unless \(c3=0\). Still **No**.

12. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + c1 + c2/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

13. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + c1 + \frac{c2}{P c3 + c4} + c5/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

14. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + P c1 + P c2 + c3 + c4/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

15. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + c1 + c2\log(P c3 + 1) + c4/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

16. \(P c0\log(P c1 + 1) + P c2 (P c3)^{c4} + P c5 + P^{c6} + c7\)  
   No forced \(P^{1/4}\) here, but structure mismatch:
   - To remove log term: set \(c0=0\).
   - Then \(P c2 (P c3)^{c4} = c2 c3^{c4} P^{1+c4}\) gives **one** power (can make \(P^2\) by \(c4=1\)).
   - \(P^{c6}\) has coefficient 1 (cannot scale), could set \(c6=1/3\) to get \(P^{1/3}\) but then coefficient is 1, whereas GTÔÇÖs \(P^{1/3}\) coefficient is \(0.857882...\) (not 1). No other term can adjust \(P^{1/3}\) coefficient without introducing extra powers. Also constant \(c7\) must be 0.  
   Cannot match all coefficients. **No**.

17. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + P c1\log(P c2 + 1) + c3 + c4/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

18. \(P^{1/4} + P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

19. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

20. \(\frac{P c0}{P c1 + 1} + P c2 + c3 + c4 \frac{t}{(P+c5)^5}\)  
   Has \(t\)-dependence unless \(c4=0\). Then still has rational \(\frac{P c0}{P c1+1}\) which cannot equal a quadratic-plus-\(P^{1/3}\) on any plausible continuous domain except degenerate cases; also no \(P^{1/3}\) term at all. **No**.

21. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + \frac{P c1}{P c2 + 1} + c3 + c4/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

22. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + P c1 + c2\log(P c3 + 1) + c4 + c5/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\). **No**.

23. \(P^{1/4} + P c0 + c1 + c2 \frac{t}{c3 t + c4} + \frac{c5}{c3 t + c4} + c6/P^{1/3}\)  
   Unavoidable \(P^{1/4}\) and \(P^{-1/3}\); also \(t\)-dependence unless \(c2=c5=0\). Still **No**.

24. \(P c0\log(1 + c1/P) + P c2 + P^{c3} c4 + P^{c5} c6\)  
   Could set \(c0=0\) to remove log. Then you have linear term plus **two** power terms \(c4 P^{c3}\) and \(c6 P^{c5}\). You could choose \(c3=2\) and \(c5=1/3\) to match the powers, and tune \(c4,c6,c2\) to match coefficients.  
   Problem: GT has **no separate pure \(P\) term beyond the combined linear coefficient**, but thatÔÇÖs fine because \(P c2\) can represent the linear coefficient. This candidate actually can represent \(A P^2 + B P + C P^{1/3}\) exactly by:
   - \(c0=0\)
   - \(c3=2,\; c4=A\)
   - \(c5=1/3,\; c6=C\)
   - \(c2=B\)
   No extra constant term. Domain condition: for real \(P^{1/3}\) as a real function, a plausible restriction is \(P\ge 0\) (or define real cube root for all reals; either way plausible).

I need to first simplify the Ground Truth (GT) expression to understand its structure.

**GT expression:**
`-6.216849410245645*1.4127513976416965*P + 0.8578822735168387*(1 - P/79.20259671838578)*P + 0.8578822735168387*P**0.333333333333333 + 0.8578822735168387*P`

Let me compute the constants:
- `-6.216849410245645 * 1.4127513976416965 Ôëł -8.7834` (coefficient of P from first term)
- `0.8578822735168387 * 1 * P = 0.8578P` (from second term, linear part)
- `0.8578822735168387 * (-P/79.20259671838578) * P = -0.01083 * P┬▓` (from second term, quadratic part)
- `0.8578822735168387 * P^(1/3)` (third term)
- `0.8578822735168387 * P` (fourth term)

Combining linear P terms: `-8.7834P + 0.8578P + 0.8578P = -7.0678P`

So GT simplifies to:
**GT = -0.01083*P┬▓ - 7.0678*P + 0.8579*P^(1/3)**

Key features of GT:
- P┬▓ term (quadratic)
- P term (linear)
- P^(1/3) term
- **No constant term** (but we could check... actually there's no explicit constant)
- **No dependence on t**
- **No P^(1/4) term**
- **No 1/P^(1/3) term**

Wait, let me re-examine. The GT has P^(1/3), not P^(1/4) or 1/P^(1/3). Many candidates have P^(1/4) and/or 1/P^(1/3) which are different basis functions.

So GT = a*P┬▓ + b*P + c*P^(1/3) where a Ôëł -0.01083, b Ôëł -7.0678, c Ôëł 0.8579, and no constant term (though we could allow a constant = 0).

Now let me check each candidate for structural compatibility. A candidate matches if it can be reduced to the form: `a*P┬▓ + b*P + c*P^(1/3) + d` where d can be 0, and has no t-dependence.

**Candidates with P^(1/4):** 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 8, 9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14, 15, 17, 18, 19, 21, 22, 23, 26, 27, 28, 38, 49
- P^(1/4) is linearly independent from P^(1/3). These cannot match unless P^(1/4) has coefficient 0, but it appears as a standalone term (coefficient 1, not adjustable). **All these are NO MATCH.**

Wait, let me check - in candidates like "P**(1/4) + P**2*c0 + ...", the P^(1/4) has coefficient 1 (fixed), not a free constant. So it cannot be zeroed out. These are all NO MATCH.

**Candidates with 1/P^(1/3):** Same issue - 1/P^(1/3) = P^(-1/3) is independent from P^(1/3).

Now checking remaining candidates without P^(1/4):

**Candidate 7:** `P*c0 + P**c1 + c2 + c3*exp(P*c4)*log(P*c5 + 1) + c6/P**(1/3)`
